info:Comfortable king-size room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Other
info:5 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 8, 2024
msg:This time I came to Changshu, Yukun Licheng Hua Ting Hotel left me a very deep impression.
From the moment I stepped into the hotel, I could feel its height, size, elegance, and comfort. The overall design of the hotel is elegant and luxurious.
The room is clean and tidy, with complete facilities. Whether it is air conditioning, TV or sanitary products, there is a sense of luxury everywhere.
The most important thing is that the hotel's service is very good. I need to sleep on a harder mattress due to lumbar disc herniation. The staff immediately came to replace the mattress for me, which makes people feel particularly considerate.
In addition, the hotel's geographical location is also very convenient. The hotel's ground and underground parking lots can fully meet your parking needs. The surrounding supporting facilities are complete, which is very convenient for travel and shopping.
The hotel's buffet breakfast is also very rich, and you can also taste Changshu's very famous Tanyou noodles and Yukun big meat buns.
In general, Yukun Hotel has performed well in all aspects. It is a very cost-effective listed five-star hotel and is worth recommending to everyone.

The TV does not have an HDMI interface. It looks like it is old at first glance. There are obvious signs of wear and tear on the hardware facilities.
